  "content": "# Istio Control Plane Developer Onboarding Guide\n\nWelcome to the Istio control plane development community! This guide will help you understand how to build Istio, navigate the codebase, and make your first contribution.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)\n2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)\n3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)\n\n---\n\n## Build Prerequisites\n\n### Required Tools and Environment\n\n**Go Version:** 1.25.0 or later\n- Install from [golang.org](https://golang.org/dl/)\n- Verify: `go version`\n\n**System Requirements:**\n- Linux, macOS, or Windows with WSL2\n- git\n- make\n- Docker (optional, for `BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=1`)\n\n**Essential Environment Variables:**\n\nThe build system automatically sets these via `common/scripts/setup_env.sh`, but you should be aware of them:\n\n- `GOPATH`: Your Go workspace directory (defaults to `../../../` relative to repo root)\n- `GO111MODULE`: Set to `on` (default)\n- `GOPROXY`: Go module proxy (defaults to `https://proxy.golang.org`)\n- `TARGET_OUT`: Build output directory (defaults to `out/linux_amd64`)\n- `TARGET_OUT_LINUX`: Linux-specific output (defaults to `out/linux_amd64`)\n- `HUB`: Docker registry for images (defaults to `istio`)\n- `TAG`: Image tag (defaults to git SHA)\n\n### Cloning the Repository\n\n```bash\n# Clone with all submodules\ngit clone --recursive https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\n\n# If you forgot --recursive, initialize submodules:\ngit submodule update --init --recursive\n```\n\n### Understanding the Build System\n\nIstio uses a Makefile-based build system with optional Docker containerization:\n\n- **`Makefile`**: Top-level entry point that delegates to `Makefile.core.mk`\n- **`Makefile.core.mk`**: Core build rules and targets\n- **`common/scripts/setup_env.sh`**: Automatically configures environment variables\n- **`BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER`**: Set to `1` to build inside Docker (only dependencies: make + docker)\n\n**Building with local toolchain (recommended for development):**\n\n```bash\n# Set up environment\nexport BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=0\n\n# Build all binaries\nmake build\n\n# Build just pilot-discovery (the main control plane)\nmake pilot-discovery\n\n# Build for Linux specifically\nmake build-linux\n```\n\n**Building in Docker container (for consistency across machines):**\n\n```bash\nexport BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=1\nmake build\n```\n\n### Core Binaries\n\nThe main control plane binary is **istiod** (called `pilot-discovery` in the codebase):\n\n- **Path**: `pilot/cmd/pilot-discovery/`\n- **Output**: `${TARGET_OUT}/pilot-discovery` or `${TARGET_OUT_LINUX}/pilot-discovery`\n- **Function**: Main Istio control plane that provides service discovery, configuration management, and certificate distribution\n\nOther important binaries:\n- **`pilot-agent`**: Data plane agent (runs on each sidecar pod/VM)\n- **`istioctl`**: Command-line tool for interacting with Istio\n- **`ztunnel`**: Ambient mesh data plane (in Rust, separate repository)\n\n### Running Tests\n\n**Unit tests:**\n\n```bash\n# Run all unit tests with race detector\nmake test\n\n# Run tests for a specific package\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\ngo test -race ./security/pkg/...\n\n# Run with verbose output\ngo test -race -v ./pilot/pkg/...\n```\n\n**Integration tests (requires Kubernetes cluster):**\n\n```bash\n# Run integration tests\nmake test.integration.kube\n\n# Run specific integration test suite\nmake test.integration.pilot.kube\nmake test.integration.security.kube\n\n# Presubmit integration tests\nmake test.integration.kube.presubmit\n```\n\n**Linting:**\n\n```bash\n# Run all linters\nmake lint\n\n# Linters include: Go linting, Python, copyright banners, Dockerfiles, YAML, Helm charts\n\n# Pre-commit checks (run before submitting PR)\nmake precommit\n\n# Auto-format code\nmake format\n```\n\n**Checking generated code:**\n\n```bash\n# Verify generated files are up to date\nmake gen-check\n\n# Update generated files\nmake gen\n```\n\n---\n\n## Architecture Overview\n\n### The Monolithic Control Plane: Istiod\n\nIstio's control plane, **istiod** (formerly split into Pilot, Citadel, and Galley), is a modular monolith containing:\n\n- **Pilot**: Service discovery, proxy configuration (xDS)\n- **Citadel**: Certificate authority and security (PKI)\n- **Galley**: Configuration management (now merged)\n- **Controllers**: Kubernetes watchers, webhook handlers, multicluster orchestration\n\n### High-Level Data Flow: Service Discovery to xDS Push\n\nHere's how the control plane goes from detecting a new service to pushing configuration to proxies:\n\n```\n1. SERVICE DISCOVERY (Input)\n   \u2193\n   Kubernetes API Server\n   \u251c\u2500 Services\n   \u251c\u2500 Endpoints\n   \u251c\u2500 Pods\n   \u2514\u2500 Custom Resources (VirtualService, Gateway, etc.)\n\n2. SERVICE REGISTRY (Aggregation Layer)\n   \u2193\n   ServiceDiscovery interface:\n   \u251c\u2500 Kube Controller (watches K8s resources)\n   \u251c\u2500 ServiceEntry Controller (watches Istio CRDs)\n   \u2514\u2500 Memory Registry (in-memory for testing)\n\n3. CONFIGURATION STORE (Input Processing)\n   \u2193\n   ConfigStore interface:\n   \u251c\u2500 CRD Client (Istio configs: VirtualService, DestinationRule)\n   \u251c\u2500 XDS Store (external xDS configs)\n   \u251c\u2500 File Store (local YAML files)\n   \u2514\u2500 Memory Store (in-memory for testing)\n\n4. PUSH CONTEXT (Snapshot)\n   \u2193\n   Immutable snapshot of current world state:\n   \u251c\u2500 Services index\n   \u251c\u2500 Endpoints index\n   \u251c\u2500 Config indexes\n   \u2514\u2500 Derived routing rules\n\n5. CONFIG GENERATORS (Translation)\n   \u2193\n   Transform Istio config \u2192 Envoy protobuf:\n   \u251c\u2500 CDS Generator \u2192 Clusters\n   \u251c\u2500 RDS Generator \u2192 HTTP Routes\n   \u251c\u2500 LDS Generator \u2192 Listeners\n   \u251c\u2500 EDS Generator \u2192 Endpoints\n   \u251c\u2500 SDS Generator \u2192 Secrets\n   \u2514\u2500 Others (ECDS, PCDS, etc.)\n\n6. XDS SERVER (Output)\n   \u2193\n   gRPC server pushes to connected proxies:\n   \u251c\u2500 Full pushes (complete config refresh)\n   \u251c\u2500 Partial pushes (incremental updates)\n   \u2514\u2500 Delta pushes (only changed resources)\n\n7. ENVOY PROXIES (Consumption)\n   \u2193\n   Sidecar/Ingress/Ztunnel receives and applies config\n```\n\n### Key Packages and Their Roles\n\n#### Pilot (Service Discovery & Proxy Configuration)\n\n**`pilot/pkg/xds/`** - XDS Protocol Implementation\n- Core discovery server managing gRPC connections from proxies\n- Handles resource generation for all xDS types\n- Key files:\n  - `discovery.go`: Main DiscoveryServer managing connections\n  - `ads.go`: ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) protocol handling\n  - `delta.go`: Delta xDS optimization\n  - Generators: `cds.go`, `rds.go`, `lds.go`, `eds.go`, `sds.go`, `ecds.go`\n\n**`pilot/pkg/networking/`** - Proxy Configuration Generation\n- Translates Istio resources into Envoy configuration\n- Key packages:\n  - `core/configgen.go`: Main ConfigGenerator interface\n  - `core/cluster_builder.go`: Builds Envoy Clusters (CDS)\n  - `core/listener_builder.go`: Builds Envoy Listeners (LDS)\n  - `core/route.go`: Builds HTTP Routes (RDS)\n  - Handles routing rules, traffic management, telemetry\n\n**`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/`** - Service Discovery Abstraction\n- Provides unified ServiceDiscovery interface over multiple backends\n- Aggregates Kubernetes services and Istio ServiceEntries\n- Sub-packages:\n  - `kube/`: Kubernetes controller and service watcher\n  - `serviceentry/`: Istio ServiceEntry resource controller\n  - `aggregate/`: Merges multiple registries\n  - `memory/`: In-memory registry (testing)\n\n**`pilot/pkg/model/`** - Core Data Structures\n- `Proxy`: Represents connected proxy (sidecar, ingress, ztunnel)\n- `Service`: Represents a mesh service\n- `ServiceInstance`: Individual endpoint of a service\n- `PushRequest`, `PushContext`: Push semantics\n- `XdsResourceGenerator`: Interface for all resource generators\n\n#### Security (Certificate Management)\n\n**`security/pkg/`** - Certificate Authority and Authentication\n- PKI management and certificate signing\n- `security/pkg/pki/`: Root CA and certificate generation\n- `security/pkg/k8s/`: Kubernetes integration for secrets\n- `security/pkg/nodeagent/`: Agent for workload certificate management\n- Integrates with pilot for mTLS configuration\n\n#### Configuration Management\n\n**`pkg/config/`** - Configuration Schema and Validation\n- Defines all Istio custom resource types (CRDs)\n- Schema validation and type marshaling\n- Used by both controllers and generators\n\n**`pkg/bootstrap/`** - Server Initialization\n- `bootstrap/server.go`: Server startup and initialization\n- Sets up all controllers, registries, webhooks\n- Initializes discovery service and security components\n\n### Understanding the Request/Response Flow\n\n#### When a Proxy Connects (e.g., new sidecar pod):\n\n1. **Proxy opens gRPC connection** to istiod on port 15010 (insecure) or 15012 (secure)\n2. **DiscoveryServer accepts connection** \u2192 creates Connection object tracking state\n3. **Proxy sends DiscoveryRequest** (e.g., for Cluster resources)\n4. **DiscoveryServer calls appropriate Generator** (e.g., CdsGenerator)\n5. **Generator reads PushContext** and proxy-specific labels\n6. **Generator constructs Envoy protobuf messages**\n7. **DiscoveryServer sends DiscoveryResponse** back to proxy\n8. **Proxy loads configuration** and starts routing traffic\n\n#### When Configuration Changes (e.g., new VirtualService):\n\n1. **Kubernetes API watchers detect change** \u2192 ConfigStore notified\n2. **ConfigStore triggers Config Update event**\n3. **Update gets debounced** (batched) for efficiency\n4. **PushContext recomputed** from new ConfigStore state\n5. **All connected proxies evaluated**: \"does this change affect me?\"\n6. **For affected proxies, generators re-run** for impacted resource types\n7. **XDS pushes sent** to proxies in queue\n\n### Optimization Layers\n\nIstiod uses several optimizations to handle thousands of proxies:\n\n1. **Debouncing**: Configuration changes batched over ~100ms\n2. **Partial PushContext**: Reuse unchanged parts (e.g., if only endpoints changed)\n3. **Per-Proxy Filtering**: Skip proxies unaffected by change\n4. **Per-Type Optimization**: Skip resource types unaffected by change (e.g., WasmPlugin doesn't affect CDS)\n5. **Partial Updates**: For non-root resources, send only changed endpoints (not full list)\n6. **Caching**: Generated protobuf cached per resource per proxy profile\n7. **Delta XDS**: Send only additions/deletions (less common, SotW preferred)\n\n### Service Registry Integration Example\n\nWhen a Kubernetes Service is created with label `app=reviews`:\n\n```\n1. Kube Controller watches Services\n   \u2193\n2. Creates model.Service with Hostname \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n   \u2193\n3. Watches corresponding Endpoints for IPs\n   \u2193\n4. Creates model.ServiceInstance for each endpoint IP+port\n   \u2193\n5. Aggregate registry merges with ServiceEntry resources\n   \u2193\n6. PushContext indexes services by hostname (for fast lookup)\n   \u2193\n7. When proxies request EDS for \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n   \u2193\n8. EDS Generator looks up service \u2192 gets endpoints \u2192 creates Envoy ClusterLoadAssignment\n   \u2193\n9. PushContext triggers XDS push to all affected proxies\n```\n\nKey file: `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go` - implements the Kube Controller that watches Kubernetes resources.\n\n---\n\n## First Contribution Workflow\n\n### Finding Good First Issues\n\nStart with issues labeled:\n- `good first issue`\n- `help wanted`\n- `area/pilot` or `area/security` for control plane work\n\nSearch in: [github.com/istio/istio/issues](https://github.com/istio/istio/issues)\n\nGood first contribution ideas:\n- Adding metrics to Pilot components\n- Improving error messages\n- Writing unit tests for existing code\n- Fixing lint issues\n- Improving documentation\n\n### Setting Up Your Development Environment\n\n```bash\n# Clone and set up\ngit clone https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\n\n# Create a feature branch\ngit checkout -b feature/my-feature-name\n\n# Verify build works\nmake build\n\n# Verify tests pass\nmake test PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...  # Test the xDS package\n```\n\n### Making Your Change\n\n**Example: Adding a metric to track xDS pushes**\n\n1. **Find the right location**:\n   - Search: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` (main discovery server)\n   - Look for where pushes happen\n\n2. **Understand existing patterns**:\n   - Read `pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go:pushXds()` to see where to add metric\n   - Check `pkg/monitoring/` for metric types\n\n3. **Make the change**:\n   ```go\n   // In pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go\n   func (s *DiscoveryServer) pushXds(con *Connection, ...) error {\n       // Add metric\n       pushXdsMetrics.WithLabelValues(\n           w.TypeUrl,\n           con.proxy.Type.String(),\n       ).Inc()\n\n       // ... rest of implementation\n   }\n   ```\n\n4. **Write/update tests**:\n   ```bash\n   # Find existing tests\n   find pilot/pkg/xds -name \"*_test.go\"\n\n   # Add test case\n   vim pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen_test.go\n\n   # Run tests\n   go test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n   ```\n\n### Running Pre-Commit Checks\n\nBefore submitting your PR:\n\n```bash\n# Format code\nmake format\n\n# Run linters (Go, Python, copyright, YAML, etc.)\nmake lint\n\n# Run tests on modified packages\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Verify no generated files changed unexpectedly\nmake gen-check\n```\n\n### Running Integration Tests\n\nFor changes affecting control plane behavior:\n\n```bash\n# Requires running Kubernetes cluster\n# Set up kind/minikube/real cluster first\n\n# Run integration tests for pilot\nmake test.integration.pilot.kube\n\n# Run security integration tests\nmake test.integration.security.kube\n\n# Run specific test\ngo test -v ./tests/integration/pilot/... -run TestName\n```\n\n### Submitting a Pull Request\n\n1. **Push your branch:**\n   ```bash\n   git add .\n   git commit -m \"feat: add xDS push metric\"\n   git push origin feature/my-feature-name\n   ```\n\n2. **Create PR on GitHub:**\n   - Title: clear summary (50 chars)\n   - Description:\n     - What changed and why\n     - Any testing performed\n     - Related issue(s): `Fixes #12345`\n   - Link to architecture docs if helpful\n\n3. **Respond to CI failures:**\n   - All tests must pass (`ci/prow/` checks)\n   - Linters must pass (`lint-go`, `lint-python`, etc.)\n   - Code coverage may be checked\n\n4. **Code Review:**\n   - Istio uses CODEOWNERS - path-based reviewer assignment\n   - Default reviewers for control plane: team members maintaining pilot, security, pkg\n   - Respond to feedback constructively\n   - Approval from two reviewers required\n\n5. **Merge:**\n   - Maintainer merges when approved and CI passes\n   - You can squash or keep commit history\n\n### Understanding Error Messages and Debugging\n\n**XDS Push Errors:**\n\n```\nlog output: \"failed to generate CDS for proxy pilot-abc123: ...\"\n```\n\nDebug by:\n1. Check what proxy properties trigger the issue: labels, namespace, cluster\n2. Add temporary `log.Debugf()` in generator\n3. Check PushContext has required data: `pilot/pkg/xds/debug.go` has debug endpoints\n4. Restart istiod and check logs\n\n**Config Generation Issues:**\n\n```\nerror: failed to convert VirtualService to Envoy config\n```\n\nDebug by:\n1. Check schema validation: `pkg/config/validation/`\n2. Test config in isolation: write unit test with your config\n3. Check generator logic: e.g., `pilot/pkg/networking/core/route.go` for RDS\n\n**Test Failures:**\n\n```bash\n# Run with more verbosity\ngo test -v -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/... -run TestDiscoveryServer\n\n# Use pprof if test hangs\ngo test -timeout 30s ./...\n```\n\n### Key Directories for Common Tasks\n\n| Task | Directory | Key Files |\n|------|-----------|-----------|\n| xDS protocol changes | `pilot/pkg/xds/` | `ads.go`, `discovery.go`, `*_gen.go` |\n| Traffic management | `pilot/pkg/networking/` | `core/configgen.go`, `core/route.go` |\n| Service discovery | `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` | `kube/controller/controller.go`, `aggregate/` |\n| Kubernetes integration | `pkg/kube/` | Controllers, client helpers |\n| Security/mTLS | `security/pkg/` | `pki/`, `nodeagent/` |\n| Configuration schema | `pkg/config/` | Type definitions, validation |\n| Tests | `pilot/test/`, `tests/integration/` | Fakes, helpers, integration tests |\n| Build | `common/scripts/`, `Makefile*` | Build scripts, make targets |\n\n### Common Development Commands\n\n```bash\n# Show make targets\nmake help\n\n# Build and test in one shot\nmake build test\n\n# Build only pilot-discovery\nmake pilot-discovery\n\n# Run specific unit test\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds -run TestDiscoveryServer -v\n\n# View test coverage\ngo test -cover ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Check linter issues\nmake lint 2>&1 | head -50\n\n# View environment variables\nmake show.env\n\n# View Go environment\nmake show.goenv\n\n# See what's being built\nmake VERBOSE=1 build\n\n# Debug with print statements\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds -run TestName -v 2>&1 | grep -A5 \"your debug string\"\n```\n\n### Useful Tools\n\n- **`istioctl`**: Debug and inspect control plane state\n  ```bash\n  make istioctl\n\n  # View xDS config for a proxy\n  kubectl exec -it <sidecar-pod> -c istio-proxy -- \\\n    curl localhost:15000/config_dump | jq\n  ```\n\n- **`ctrlz`** (Control-Z): Interactive debugging interface\n  - Built into istiod on port 8080\n  - View logs, metrics, environment: `http://localhost:8080`\n\n- **Go debugging**:\n  ```bash\n  # Use delve debugger\n  dlv test ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n  ```\n\n- **Metrics inspection**:\n  - Prometheus metrics on port 15014\n  - Relevant metrics: `pilot_xds_*`, `pilot_config_*`\n\n---\n\n## Resources\n\n- **[Official Istio Docs](https://istio.io/)**: User-facing documentation\n- **[Community Repository](https://github.com/istio/community)**: Contributing guidelines, RFCs, meeting notes\n- **[Architecture Docs](./architecture/)**: Deep dives into components\n  - `architecture/networking/pilot.md`: Control plane architecture\n  - `architecture/security/istio-agent.md`: Security/agent architecture\n- **[Wiki](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki)**: Development conventions, performance tips\n- **[Development Conventions](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Development-Conventions)**: Code style, naming\n- **[Project Structure](https://github.com/istio/community)**: Detailed project layout\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nYou now understand:\n\n1. \u2705 **How to build** Istio from source using the Makefile\n2. \u2705 **Core architecture** of the control plane (Istiod's components and data flows)\n3. \u2705 **Service-to-configuration journey** from Kubernetes \u2192 PushContext \u2192 Generators \u2192 xDS \u2192 Envoy\n4. \u2705 **Key packages** and where to find code for different features\n5. \u2705 **Testing workflows** for unit and integration tests\n6. \u2705 **First contribution steps** from environment setup to PR submission\n\n**Next steps:**\n- Pick a `good first issue` from GitHub\n- Run the build and tests in your environment\n- Make your first contribution! \ud83d\ude80\n\nGood luck and happy coding!\n",

  "content": "# Istio Control Plane Developer Onboarding Guide\n\nWelcome to the Istio control plane development community! This guide will help you understand how to build Istio, navigate the codebase, and make your first contribution.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)\n2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)\n3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)\n\n---\n\n## Build Prerequisites\n\n### Required Tools and Environment\n\n**Go Version:** 1.25.0 or later\n- Install from [golang.org](https://golang.org/dl/)\n- Verify: `go version`\n\n**System Requirements:**\n- Linux, macOS, or Windows with WSL2\n- git\n- make\n- Docker (optional, for `BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=1`)\n\n**Essential Environment Variables:**\n\nThe build system automatically sets these via `common/scripts/setup_env.sh`, but you should be aware of them:\n\n- `GOPATH`: Your Go workspace directory (defaults to `../../../` relative to repo root)\n- `GO111MODULE`: Set to `on` (default)\n- `GOPROXY`: Go module proxy (defaults to `https://proxy.golang.org`)\n- `TARGET_OUT`: Build output directory (defaults to `out/linux_amd64`)\n- `TARGET_OUT_LINUX`: Linux-specific output (defaults to `out/linux_amd64`)\n- `HUB`: Docker registry for images (defaults to `istio`)\n- `TAG`: Image tag (defaults to git SHA)\n\n### Cloning the Repository\n\n```bash\n# Clone with all submodules\ngit clone --recursive https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\n\n# If you forgot --recursive, initialize submodules:\ngit submodule update --init --recursive\n```\n\n### Understanding the Build System\n\nIstio uses a Makefile-based build system with optional Docker containerization:\n\n- **`Makefile`**: Top-level entry point that delegates to `Makefile.core.mk`\n- **`Makefile.core.mk`**: Core build rules and targets\n- **`common/scripts/setup_env.sh`**: Automatically configures environment variables\n- **`BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER`**: Set to `1` to build inside Docker (only dependencies: make + docker)\n\n**Building with local toolchain (recommended for development):**\n\n```bash\n# Set up environment\nexport BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=0\n\n# Build all binaries\nmake build\n\n# Build just pilot-discovery (the main control plane)\nmake pilot-discovery\n\n# Build for Linux specifically\nmake build-linux\n```\n\n**Building in Docker container (for consistency across machines):**\n\n```bash\nexport BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=1\nmake build\n```\n\n### Core Binaries\n\nThe main control plane binary is **istiod** (called `pilot-discovery` in the codebase):\n\n- **Path**: `pilot/cmd/pilot-discovery/`\n- **Output**: `${TARGET_OUT}/pilot-discovery` or `${TARGET_OUT_LINUX}/pilot-discovery`\n- **Function**: Main Istio control plane that provides service discovery, configuration management, and certificate distribution\n\nOther important binaries:\n- **`pilot-agent`**: Data plane agent (runs on each sidecar pod/VM)\n- **`istioctl`**: Command-line tool for interacting with Istio\n- **`ztunnel`**: Ambient mesh data plane (in Rust, separate repository)\n\n### Running Tests\n\n**Unit tests:**\n\n```bash\n# Run all unit tests with race detector\nmake test\n\n# Run tests for a specific package\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\ngo test -race ./security/pkg/...\n\n# Run with verbose output\ngo test -race -v ./pilot/pkg/...\n```\n\n**Integration tests (requires Kubernetes cluster):**\n\n```bash\n# Run integration tests\nmake test.integration.kube\n\n# Run specific integration test suite\nmake test.integration.pilot.kube\nmake test.integration.security.kube\n\n# Presubmit integration tests\nmake test.integration.kube.presubmit\n```\n\n**Linting:**\n\n```bash\n# Run all linters\nmake lint\n\n# Linters include: Go linting, Python, copyright banners, Dockerfiles, YAML, Helm charts\n\n# Pre-commit checks (run before submitting PR)\nmake precommit\n\n# Auto-format code\nmake format\n```\n\n**Checking generated code:**\n\n```bash\n# Verify generated files are up to date\nmake gen-check\n\n# Update generated files\nmake gen\n```\n\n---\n\n## Architecture Overview\n\n### The Monolithic Control Plane: Istiod\n\nIstio's control plane, **istiod** (formerly split into Pilot, Citadel, and Galley), is a modular monolith containing:\n\n- **Pilot**: Service discovery, proxy configuration (xDS)\n- **Citadel**: Certificate authority and security (PKI)\n- **Galley**: Configuration management (now merged)\n- **Controllers**: Kubernetes watchers, webhook handlers, multicluster orchestration\n\n### High-Level Data Flow: Service Discovery to xDS Push\n\nHere's how the control plane goes from detecting a new service to pushing configuration to proxies:\n\n```\n1. SERVICE DISCOVERY (Input)\n   \u2193\n   Kubernetes API Server\n   \u251c\u2500 Services\n   \u251c\u2500 Endpoints\n   \u251c\u2500 Pods\n   \u2514\u2500 Custom Resources (VirtualService, Gateway, etc.)\n\n2. SERVICE REGISTRY (Aggregation Layer)\n   \u2193\n   ServiceDiscovery interface:\n   \u251c\u2500 Kube Controller (watches K8s resources)\n   \u251c\u2500 ServiceEntry Controller (watches Istio CRDs)\n   \u2514\u2500 Memory Registry (in-memory for testing)\n\n3. CONFIGURATION STORE (Input Processing)\n   \u2193\n   ConfigStore interface:\n   \u251c\u2500 CRD Client (Istio configs: VirtualService, DestinationRule)\n   \u251c\u2500 XDS Store (external xDS configs)\n   \u251c\u2500 File Store (local YAML files)\n   \u2514\u2500 Memory Store (in-memory for testing)\n\n4. PUSH CONTEXT (Snapshot)\n   \u2193\n   Immutable snapshot of current world state:\n   \u251c\u2500 Services index\n   \u251c\u2500 Endpoints index\n   \u251c\u2500 Config indexes\n   \u2514\u2500 Derived routing rules\n\n5. CONFIG GENERATORS (Translation)\n   \u2193\n   Transform Istio config \u2192 Envoy protobuf:\n   \u251c\u2500 CDS Generator \u2192 Clusters\n   \u251c\u2500 RDS Generator \u2192 HTTP Routes\n   \u251c\u2500 LDS Generator \u2192 Listeners\n   \u251c\u2500 EDS Generator \u2192 Endpoints\n   \u251c\u2500 SDS Generator \u2192 Secrets\n   \u2514\u2500 Others (ECDS, PCDS, etc.)\n\n6. XDS SERVER (Output)\n   \u2193\n   gRPC server pushes to connected proxies:\n   \u251c\u2500 Full pushes (complete config refresh)\n   \u251c\u2500 Partial pushes (incremental updates)\n   \u2514\u2500 Delta pushes (only changed resources)\n\n7. ENVOY PROXIES (Consumption)\n   \u2193\n   Sidecar/Ingress/Ztunnel receives and applies config\n```\n\n### Key Packages and Their Roles\n\n#### Pilot (Service Discovery & Proxy Configuration)\n\n**`pilot/pkg/xds/`** - XDS Protocol Implementation\n- Core discovery server managing gRPC connections from proxies\n- Handles resource generation for all xDS types\n- Key files:\n  - `discovery.go`: Main DiscoveryServer managing connections\n  - `ads.go`: ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) protocol handling\n  - `delta.go`: Delta xDS optimization\n  - Generators: `cds.go`, `rds.go`, `lds.go`, `eds.go`, `sds.go`, `ecds.go`\n\n**`pilot/pkg/networking/`** - Proxy Configuration Generation\n- Translates Istio resources into Envoy configuration\n- Key packages:\n  - `core/configgen.go`: Main ConfigGenerator interface\n  - `core/cluster_builder.go`: Builds Envoy Clusters (CDS)\n  - `core/listener_builder.go`: Builds Envoy Listeners (LDS)\n  - `core/route.go`: Builds HTTP Routes (RDS)\n  - Handles routing rules, traffic management, telemetry\n\n**`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/`** - Service Discovery Abstraction\n- Provides unified ServiceDiscovery interface over multiple backends\n- Aggregates Kubernetes services and Istio ServiceEntries\n- Sub-packages:\n  - `kube/`: Kubernetes controller and service watcher\n  - `serviceentry/`: Istio ServiceEntry resource controller\n  - `aggregate/`: Merges multiple registries\n  - `memory/`: In-memory registry (testing)\n\n**`pilot/pkg/model/`** - Core Data Structures\n- `Proxy`: Represents connected proxy (sidecar, ingress, ztunnel)\n- `Service`: Represents a mesh service\n- `ServiceInstance`: Individual endpoint of a service\n- `PushRequest`, `PushContext`: Push semantics\n- `XdsResourceGenerator`: Interface for all resource generators\n\n#### Security (Certificate Management)\n\n**`security/pkg/`** - Certificate Authority and Authentication\n- PKI management and certificate signing\n- `security/pkg/pki/`: Root CA and certificate generation\n- `security/pkg/k8s/`: Kubernetes integration for secrets\n- `security/pkg/nodeagent/`: Agent for workload certificate management\n- Integrates with pilot for mTLS configuration\n\n#### Configuration Management\n\n**`pkg/config/`** - Configuration Schema and Validation\n- Defines all Istio custom resource types (CRDs)\n- Schema validation and type marshaling\n- Used by both controllers and generators\n\n**`pkg/bootstrap/`** - Server Initialization\n- `bootstrap/server.go`: Server startup and initialization\n- Sets up all controllers, registries, webhooks\n- Initializes discovery service and security components\n\n### Understanding the Request/Response Flow\n\n#### When a Proxy Connects (e.g., new sidecar pod):\n\n1. **Proxy opens gRPC connection** to istiod on port 15010 (insecure) or 15012 (secure)\n2. **DiscoveryServer accepts connection** \u2192 creates Connection object tracking state\n3. **Proxy sends DiscoveryRequest** (e.g., for Cluster resources)\n4. **DiscoveryServer calls appropriate Generator** (e.g., CdsGenerator)\n5. **Generator reads PushContext** and proxy-specific labels\n6. **Generator constructs Envoy protobuf messages**\n7. **DiscoveryServer sends DiscoveryResponse** back to proxy\n8. **Proxy loads configuration** and starts routing traffic\n\n#### When Configuration Changes (e.g., new VirtualService):\n\n1. **Kubernetes API watchers detect change** \u2192 ConfigStore notified\n2. **ConfigStore triggers Config Update event**\n3. **Update gets debounced** (batched) for efficiency\n4. **PushContext recomputed** from new ConfigStore state\n5. **All connected proxies evaluated**: \"does this change affect me?\"\n6. **For affected proxies, generators re-run** for impacted resource types\n7. **XDS pushes sent** to proxies in queue\n\n### Optimization Layers\n\nIstiod uses several optimizations to handle thousands of proxies:\n\n1. **Debouncing**: Configuration changes batched over ~100ms\n2. **Partial PushContext**: Reuse unchanged parts (e.g., if only endpoints changed)\n3. **Per-Proxy Filtering**: Skip proxies unaffected by change\n4. **Per-Type Optimization**: Skip resource types unaffected by change (e.g., WasmPlugin doesn't affect CDS)\n5. **Partial Updates**: For non-root resources, send only changed endpoints (not full list)\n6. **Caching**: Generated protobuf cached per resource per proxy profile\n7. **Delta XDS**: Send only additions/deletions (less common, SotW preferred)\n\n### Service Registry Integration Example\n\nWhen a Kubernetes Service is created with label `app=reviews`:\n\n```\n1. Kube Controller watches Services\n   \u2193\n2. Creates model.Service with Hostname \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n   \u2193\n3. Watches corresponding Endpoints for IPs\n   \u2193\n4. Creates model.ServiceInstance for each endpoint IP+port\n   \u2193\n5. Aggregate registry merges with ServiceEntry resources\n   \u2193\n6. PushContext indexes services by hostname (for fast lookup)\n   \u2193\n7. When proxies request EDS for \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n   \u2193\n8. EDS Generator looks up service \u2192 gets endpoints \u2192 creates Envoy ClusterLoadAssignment\n   \u2193\n9. PushContext triggers XDS push to all affected proxies\n```\n\nKey file: `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go` - implements the Kube Controller that watches Kubernetes resources.\n\n---\n\n## First Contribution Workflow\n\n### Finding Good First Issues\n\nStart with issues labeled:\n- `good first issue`\n- `help wanted`\n- `area/pilot` or `area/security` for control plane work\n\nSearch in: [github.com/istio/istio/issues](https://github.com/istio/istio/issues)\n\nGood first contribution ideas:\n- Adding metrics to Pilot components\n- Improving error messages\n- Writing unit tests for existing code\n- Fixing lint issues\n- Improving documentation\n\n### Setting Up Your Development Environment\n\n```bash\n# Clone and set up\ngit clone https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\n\n# Create a feature branch\ngit checkout -b feature/my-feature-name\n\n# Verify build works\nmake build\n\n# Verify tests pass\nmake test PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...  # Test the xDS package\n```\n\n### Making Your Change\n\n**Example: Adding a metric to track xDS pushes**\n\n1. **Find the right location**:\n   - Search: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` (main discovery server)\n   - Look for where pushes happen\n\n2. **Understand existing patterns**:\n   - Read `pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go:pushXds()` to see where to add metric\n   - Check `pkg/monitoring/` for metric types\n\n3. **Make the change**:\n   ```go\n   // In pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go\n   func (s *DiscoveryServer) pushXds(con *Connection, ...) error {\n       // Add metric\n       pushXdsMetrics.WithLabelValues(\n           w.TypeUrl,\n           con.proxy.Type.String(),\n       ).Inc()\n\n       // ... rest of implementation\n   }\n   ```\n\n4. **Write/update tests**:\n   ```bash\n   # Find existing tests\n   find pilot/pkg/xds -name \"*_test.go\"\n\n   # Add test case\n   vim pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen_test.go\n\n   # Run tests\n   go test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n   ```\n\n### Running Pre-Commit Checks\n\nBefore submitting your PR:\n\n```bash\n# Format code\nmake format\n\n# Run linters (Go, Python, copyright, YAML, etc.)\nmake lint\n\n# Run tests on modified packages\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Verify no generated files changed unexpectedly\nmake gen-check\n```\n\n### Running Integration Tests\n\nFor changes affecting control plane behavior:\n\n```bash\n# Requires running Kubernetes cluster\n# Set up kind/minikube/real cluster first\n\n# Run integration tests for pilot\nmake test.integration.pilot.kube\n\n# Run security integration tests\nmake test.integration.security.kube\n\n# Run specific test\ngo test -v ./tests/integration/pilot/... -run TestName\n```\n\n### Submitting a Pull Request\n\n1. **Push your branch:**\n   ```bash\n   git add .\n   git commit -m \"feat: add xDS push metric\"\n   git push origin feature/my-feature-name\n   ```\n\n2. **Create PR on GitHub:**\n   - Title: clear summary (50 chars)\n   - Description:\n     - What changed and why\n     - Any testing performed\n     - Related issue(s): `Fixes #12345`\n   - Link to architecture docs if helpful\n\n3. **Respond to CI failures:**\n   - All tests must pass (`ci/prow/` checks)\n   - Linters must pass (`lint-go`, `lint-python`, etc.)\n   - Code coverage may be checked\n\n4. **Code Review:**\n   - Istio uses CODEOWNERS - path-based reviewer assignment\n   - Default reviewers for control plane: team members maintaining pilot, security, pkg\n   - Respond to feedback constructively\n   - Approval from two reviewers required\n\n5. **Merge:**\n   - Maintainer merges when approved and CI passes\n   - You can squash or keep commit history\n\n### Understanding Error Messages and Debugging\n\n**XDS Push Errors:**\n\n```\nlog output: \"failed to generate CDS for proxy pilot-abc123: ...\"\n```\n\nDebug by:\n1. Check what proxy properties trigger the issue: labels, namespace, cluster\n2. Add temporary `log.Debugf()` in generator\n3. Check PushContext has required data: `pilot/pkg/xds/debug.go` has debug endpoints\n4. Restart istiod and check logs\n\n**Config Generation Issues:**\n\n```\nerror: failed to convert VirtualService to Envoy config\n```\n\nDebug by:\n1. Check schema validation: `pkg/config/validation/`\n2. Test config in isolation: write unit test with your config\n3. Check generator logic: e.g., `pilot/pkg/networking/core/route.go` for RDS\n\n**Test Failures:**\n\n```bash\n# Run with more verbosity\ngo test -v -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/... -run TestDiscoveryServer\n\n# Use pprof if test hangs\ngo test -timeout 30s ./...\n```\n\n### Key Directories for Common Tasks\n\n| Task | Directory | Key Files |\n|------|-----------|-----------|\n| xDS protocol changes | `pilot/pkg/xds/` | `ads.go`, `discovery.go`, `*_gen.go` |\n| Traffic management | `pilot/pkg/networking/` | `core/configgen.go`, `core/route.go` |\n| Service discovery | `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` | `kube/controller/controller.go`, `aggregate/` |\n| Kubernetes integration | `pkg/kube/` | Controllers, client helpers |\n| Security/mTLS | `security/pkg/` | `pki/`, `nodeagent/` |\n| Configuration schema | `pkg/config/` | Type definitions, validation |\n| Tests | `pilot/test/`, `tests/integration/` | Fakes, helpers, integration tests |\n| Build | `common/scripts/`, `Makefile*` | Build scripts, make targets |\n\n### Common Development Commands\n\n```bash\n# Show make targets\nmake help\n\n# Build and test in one shot\nmake build test\n\n# Build only pilot-discovery\nmake pilot-discovery\n\n# Run specific unit test\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds -run TestDiscoveryServer -v\n\n# View test coverage\ngo test -cover ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Check linter issues\nmake lint 2>&1 | head -50\n\n# View environment variables\nmake show.env\n\n# View Go environment\nmake show.goenv\n\n# See what's being built\nmake VERBOSE=1 build\n\n# Debug with print statements\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds -run TestName -v 2>&1 | grep -A5 \"your debug string\"\n```\n\n### Useful Tools\n\n- **`istioctl`**: Debug and inspect control plane state\n  ```bash\n  make istioctl\n\n  # View xDS config for a proxy\n  kubectl exec -it <sidecar-pod> -c istio-proxy -- \\\n    curl localhost:15000/config_dump | jq\n  ```\n\n- **`ctrlz`** (Control-Z): Interactive debugging interface\n  - Built into istiod on port 8080\n  - View logs, metrics, environment: `http://localhost:8080`\n\n- **Go debugging**:\n  ```bash\n  # Use delve debugger\n  dlv test ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n  ```\n\n- **Metrics inspection**:\n  - Prometheus metrics on port 15014\n  - Relevant metrics: `pilot_xds_*`, `pilot_config_*`\n\n---\n\n## Resources\n\n- **[Official Istio Docs](https://istio.io/)**: User-facing documentation\n- **[Community Repository](https://github.com/istio/community)**: Contributing guidelines, RFCs, meeting notes\n- **[Architecture Docs](./architecture/)**: Deep dives into components\n  - `architecture/networking/pilot.md`: Control plane architecture\n  - `architecture/security/istio-agent.md`: Security/agent architecture\n- **[Wiki](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki)**: Development conventions, performance tips\n- **[Development Conventions](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Development-Conventions)**: Code style, naming\n- **[Project Structure](https://github.com/istio/community)**: Detailed project layout\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nYou now understand:\n\n1. \u2705 **How to build** Istio from source using the Makefile\n2. \u2705 **Core architecture** of the control plane (Istiod's components and data flows)\n3. \u2705 **Service-to-configuration journey** from Kubernetes \u2192 PushContext \u2192 Generators \u2192 xDS \u2192 Envoy\n4. \u2705 **Key packages** and where to find code for different features\n5. \u2705 **Testing workflows** for unit and integration tests\n6. \u2705 **First contribution steps** from environment setup to PR submission\n\n**Next steps:**\n- Pick a `good first issue` from GitHub\n- Run the build and tests in your environment\n- Make your first contribution! \ud83d\ude80\n\nGood luck and happy coding!\n",

CONFIGURATION STORE (Input Processing)\n   \u2193\n   ConfigStore interface:\n   \u251c\u2500 CRD Client (Istio configs: VirtualService, DestinationRule)\n   \u251c\u2500 XDS Store (external xDS configs)\n   \u251c\u2500 File Store (local YAML files)\n   \u2514\u2500 Memory Store (in-memory for testing)\n\n4. PUSH CONTEXT (Snapshot)\n   \u2193\n   Immutable snapshot of current world state:\n   \u251c\u2500 Services index\n   \u251c\u2500 Endpoints index\n   \u251c\u2500 Config indexes\n   \u2514\u2500 Derived routing rules\n\n5. CONFIG GENERATORS (Translation)\n   \u2193\n   Transform Istio config \u2192 Envoy protobuf:\n   \u251c\u2500 CDS Generator \u2192 Clusters\n   \u251c\u2500 RDS Generator \u2192 HTTP Routes\n   \u251c\u2500 LDS Generator \u2192 Listeners\n   \u251c\u2500 EDS Generator \u2192 Endpoints\n   \u251c\u2500 SDS Generator \u2192 Secrets\n   \u2514\u2500 Others (ECDS, PCDS, etc.)\n\n6. XDS SERVER (Output)\n   \u2193\n   gRPC server pushes to connected proxies:\n   \u251c\u2500 Full pushes (complete config refresh)\n   \u251c\u2500 Partial pushes (incremental updates)\n   \u2514\u2500 Delta pushes (only changed resources)\n\n7. ENVOY PROXIES (Consumption)\n   \u2193\n   Sidecar/Ingress/Ztunnel receives and applies config\n```\n\n### Key Packages and Their Roles\n\n#### Pilot (Service Discovery & Proxy Configuration)\n\n**`pilot/pkg/xds/`** - XDS Protocol Implementation\n- Core discovery server managing gRPC connections from proxies\n- Handles resource generation for all xDS types\n- Key files:\n  - `discovery.go`: Main DiscoveryServer managing connections\n  - `ads.go`: ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) protocol handling\n  - `delta.go`: Delta xDS optimization\n  - Generators: `cds.go`, `rds.go`, `lds.go`, `eds.go`, `sds.go`, `ecds.go`\n\n**`pilot/pkg/networking/`** - Proxy Configuration Generation\n- Translates Istio resources into Envoy configuration\n- Key packages:\n  - `core/configgen.go`: Main ConfigGenerator interface\n  - `core/cluster_builder.go`: Builds Envoy Clusters (CDS)\n  - `core/listener_builder.go`: Builds Envoy Listeners (LDS)\n  - `core/route.go`: Builds HTTP Routes (RDS)\n  - Handles routing rules, traffic management, telemetry\n\n**`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/`** - Service Discovery Abstraction\n- Provides unified ServiceDiscovery interface over multiple backends\n- Aggregates Kubernetes services and Istio ServiceEntries\n- Sub-packages:\n  - `kube/`: Kubernetes controller and service watcher\n  - `serviceentry/`: Istio ServiceEntry resource controller\n  - `aggregate/`: Merges multiple registries\n  - `memory/`: In-memory registry (testing)\n\n**`pilot/pkg/model/`** - Core Data Structures\n- `Proxy`: Represents connected proxy (sidecar, ingress, ztunnel)\n- `Service`: Represents a mesh service\n- `ServiceInstance`: Individual endpoint of a service\n- `PushRequest`, `PushContext`: Push semantics\n- `XdsResourceGenerator`: Interface for all resource generators\n\n#### Security (Certificate Management)\n\n**`security/pkg/`** - Certificate Authority and Authentication\n- PKI management and certificate signing\n- `security/pkg/pki/`: Root CA and certificate generation\n- `security/pkg/k8s/`: Kubernetes integration for secrets\n- `security/pkg/nodeagent/`: Agent for workload certificate management\n- Integrates with pilot for mTLS configuration\n\n#### Configuration Management\n\n**`pkg/config/`** - Configuration Schema and Validation\n- Defines all Istio custom resource types (CRDs)\n- Schema validation and type marshaling\n- Used by both controllers and generators\n\n**`pkg/bootstrap/`** - Server Initialization\n- `bootstrap/server.go`: Server startup and initialization\n- Sets up all controllers, registries, webhooks\n- Initializes discovery service and security components\n\n### Understanding the Request/Response Flow\n\n#### When a Proxy Connects (e.g., new sidecar pod):\n\n1. **Proxy opens gRPC connection** to istiod on port 15010 (insecure) or 15012 (secure)\n2. **DiscoveryServer accepts connection** \u2192 creates Connection object tracking state\n3. **Proxy sends DiscoveryRequest** (e.g., for Cluster resources)\n4. **DiscoveryServer calls appropriate Generator** (e.g., CdsGenerator)\n5. **Generator reads PushContext** and proxy-specific labels\n6. **Generator constructs Envoy protobuf messages**\n7. **DiscoveryServer sends DiscoveryResponse** back to proxy\n8. **Proxy loads configuration** and starts routing traffic\n\n#### When Configuration Changes (e.g., new VirtualService):\n\n1. **Kubernetes API watchers detect change** \u2192 ConfigStore notified\n2. **ConfigStore triggers Config Update event**\n3. **Update gets debounced** (batched) for efficiency\n4. **PushContext recomputed** from new ConfigStore state\n5. **All connected proxies evaluated**: \"does this change affect me?\"\n6. **For affected proxies, generators re-run** for impacted resource types\n7. **XDS pushes sent** to proxies in queue\n\n### Optimization Layers\n\nIstiod uses several optimizations to handle thousands of proxies:\n\n1. **Debouncing**: Configuration changes batched over ~100ms\n2. **Partial PushContext**: Reuse unchanged parts (e.g., if only endpoints changed)\n3. **Per-Proxy Filtering**: Skip proxies unaffected by change\n4. **Per-Type Optimization**: Skip resource types unaffected by change (e.g., WasmPlugin doesn't affect CDS)\n5. **Partial Updates**: For non-root resources, send only changed endpoints (not full list)\n6. **Caching**: Generated protobuf cached per resource per proxy profile\n7. **Delta XDS**: Send only additions/deletions (less common, SotW preferred)\n\n### Service Registry Integration Example\n\nWhen a Kubernetes Service is created with label `app=reviews`:\n\n```\n1. Kube Controller watches Services\n   \u2193\n2. Creates model.Service with Hostname \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n   \u2193\n3. Watches corresponding Endpoints for IPs\n   \u2193\n4. Creates model.ServiceInstance for each endpoint IP+port\n   \u2193\n5. Aggregate registry merges with ServiceEntry resources\n   \u2193\n6. PushContext indexes services by hostname (for fast lookup)\n   \u2193\n7. When proxies request EDS for \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n   \u2193\n8. EDS Generator looks up service \u2192 gets endpoints \u2192 creates Envoy ClusterLoadAssignment\n   \u2193\n9. PushContext triggers XDS push to all affected proxies\n```\n\nKey file: `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go` - implements the Kube Controller that watches Kubernetes resources.\n\n---\n\n## First Contribution Workflow\n\n### Finding Good First Issues\n\nStart with issues labeled:\n- `good first issue`\n- `help wanted`\n- `area/pilot` or `area/security` for control plane work\n\nSearch in: [github.com/istio/istio/issues](https://github.com/istio/istio/issues)\n\nGood first contribution ideas:\n- Adding metrics to Pilot components\n- Improving error messages\n- Writing unit tests for existing code\n- Fixing lint issues\n- Improving documentation\n\n### Setting Up Your Development Environment\n\n```bash\n# Clone and set up\ngit clone https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\n\n# Create a feature branch\ngit checkout -b feature/my-feature-name\n\n# Verify build works\nmake build\n\n# Verify tests pass\nmake test PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...  # Test the xDS package\n```\n\n### Making Your Change\n\n**Example: Adding a metric to track xDS pushes**\n\n1. **Find the right location**:\n   - Search: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` (main discovery server)\n   - Look for where pushes happen\n\n2. **Understand existing patterns**:\n   - Read `pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go:pushXds()` to see where to add metric\n   - Check `pkg/monitoring/` for metric types\n\n3. **Make the change**:\n   ```go\n   // In pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go\n   func (s *DiscoveryServer) pushXds(con *Connection, ...) error {\n       // Add metric\n       pushXdsMetrics.WithLabelValues(\n           w.TypeUrl,\n           con.proxy.Type.String(),\n       ).Inc()\n\n       // ... rest of implementation\n   }\n   ```\n\n4. **Write/update tests**:\n   ```bash\n   # Find existing tests\n   find pilot/pkg/xds -name \"*_test.go\"\n\n   # Add test case\n   vim pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen_test.go\n\n   # Run tests\n   go test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n   ```\n\n### Running Pre-Commit Checks\n\nBefore submitting your PR:\n\n```bash\n# Format code\nmake format\n\n# Run linters (Go, Python, copyright, YAML, etc.)\nmake lint\n\n# Run tests on modified packages\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Verify no generated files changed unexpectedly\nmake gen-check\n```\n\n### Running Integration Tests\n\nFor changes affecting control plane behavior:\n\n```bash\n# Requires running Kubernetes cluster\n# Set up kind/minikube/real cluster first\n\n# Run integration tests for pilot\nmake test.integration.pilot.kube\n\n# Run security integration tests\nmake test.integration.security.kube\n\n# Run specific test\ngo test -v ./tests/integration/pilot/... -run TestName\n```\n\n### Submitting a Pull Request\n\n1. **Push your branch:**\n   ```bash\n   git add .\n   git commit -m \"feat: add xDS push metric\"\n   git push origin feature/my-feature-name\n   ```\n\n2. **Create PR on GitHub:**\n   - Title: clear summary (50 chars)\n   - Description:\n     - What changed and why\n     - Any testing performed\n     - Related issue(s): `Fixes #12345`\n   - Link to architecture docs if helpful\n\n3. **Respond to CI failures:**\n   - All tests must pass (`ci/prow/` checks)\n   - Linters must pass (`lint-go`, `lint-python`, etc.)\n   - Code coverage may be checked\n\n4. **Code Review:**\n   - Istio uses CODEOWNERS - path-based reviewer assignment\n   - Default reviewers for control plane: team members maintaining pilot, security, pkg\n   - Respond to feedback constructively\n   - Approval from two reviewers required\n\n5. **Merge:**\n   - Maintainer merges when approved and CI passes\n   - You can squash or keep commit history\n\n### Understanding Error Messages and Debugging\n\n**XDS Push Errors:**\n\n```\nlog output: \"failed to generate CDS for proxy pilot-abc123: ...\"\n```\n\nDebug by:\n1. Check what proxy properties trigger the issue: labels, namespace, cluster\n2. Add temporary `log.Debugf()` in generator\n3. Check PushContext has required data: `pilot/pkg/xds/debug.go` has debug endpoints\n4. Restart istiod and check logs\n\n**Config Generation Issues:**\n\n```\nerror: failed to convert VirtualService to Envoy config\n```\n\nDebug by:\n1. Check schema validation: `pkg/config/validation/`\n2. Test config in isolation: write unit test with your config\n3. Check generator logic: e.g., `pilot/pkg/networking/core/route.go` for RDS\n\n**Test Failures:**\n\n```bash\n# Run with more verbosity\ngo test -v -race ./pilot/pkg/xds/... -run TestDiscoveryServer\n\n# Use pprof if test hangs\ngo test -timeout 30s ./...\n```\n\n### Key Directories for Common Tasks\n\n| Task | Directory | Key Files |\n|------|-----------|-----------|\n| xDS protocol changes | `pilot/pkg/xds/` | `ads.go`, `discovery.go`, `*_gen.go` |\n| Traffic management | `pilot/pkg/networking/` | `core/configgen.go`, `core/route.go` |\n| Service discovery | `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` | `kube/controller/controller.go`, `aggregate/` |\n| Kubernetes integration | `pkg/kube/` | Controllers, client helpers |\n| Security/mTLS | `security/pkg/` | `pki/`, `nodeagent/` |\n| Configuration schema | `pkg/config/` | Type definitions, validation |\n| Tests | `pilot/test/`, `tests/integration/` | Fakes, helpers, integration tests |\n| Build | `common/scripts/`, `Makefile*` | Build scripts, make targets |\n\n### Common Development Commands\n\n```bash\n# Show make targets\nmake help\n\n# Build and test in one shot\nmake build test\n\n# Build only pilot-discovery\nmake pilot-discovery\n\n# Run specific unit test\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds -run TestDiscoveryServer -v\n\n# View test coverage\ngo test -cover ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Check linter issues\nmake lint 2>&1 | head -50\n\n# View environment variables\nmake show.env\n\n# View Go environment\nmake show.goenv\n\n# See what's being built\nmake VERBOSE=1 build\n\n# Debug with print statements\ngo test -race ./pilot/pkg/xds -run TestName -v 2>&1 | grep -A5 \"your debug string\"\n```\n\n### Useful Tools\n\n- **`istioctl`**: Debug and inspect control plane state\n  ```bash\n  make istioctl\n\n  # View xDS config for a proxy\n  kubectl exec -it <sidecar-pod> -c istio-proxy -- \\\n    curl localhost:15000/config_dump | jq\n  ```\n\n- **`ctrlz`** (Control-Z): Interactive debugging interface\n  - Built into istiod on port 8080\n  - View logs, metrics, environment: `http://localhost:8080`\n\n- **Go debugging**:\n  ```bash\n  # Use delve debugger\n  dlv test ./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n  ```\n\n- **Metrics inspection**:\n  - Prometheus metrics on port 15014\n  - Relevant metrics: `pilot_xds_*`, `pilot_config_*`\n\n---\n\n## Resources\n\n- **[Official Istio Docs](https://istio.io/)**: User-facing documentation\n- **[Community Repository](https://github.com/istio/community)**: Contributing guidelines, RFCs, meeting notes\n- **[Architecture Docs](./architecture/)**: Deep dives into components\n  - # Istio Control Plane Developer Onboarding Guide

Welcome to the Istio control plane development community! This guide will help you understand how to build Istio, navigate the codebase, and make your first contribution.

## Table of Contents

1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)
2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)
3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)

---

## Build Prerequisites

### Required Tools and Environment

**Go Version:** 1.25.0 or later
- Install from [golang.org](https://golang.org/dl/)
- Verify: `go version`

**System Requirements:**
- Linux, macOS, or Windows with WSL2
- git
- make
- Docker (optional, for `BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=1`)

**Essential Environment Variables:**

The build system automatically sets these via `common/scripts/setup_env.sh`, but you should be aware of them:

- `GOPATH`: Your Go workspace directory (defaults to `../../../` relative to repo root)
- `GO111MODULE`: Set to `on` (default)
- `GOPROXY`: Go module proxy (defaults to `https://proxy.golang.org`)
- `TARGET_OUT`: Build output directory (defaults to `out/linux_amd64`)
- `TARGET_OUT_LINUX`: Linux-specific output (defaults to `out/linux_amd64`)
- `HUB`: Docker registry for images (defaults to `istio`)
- `TAG`: Image tag (defaults to git SHA)

### Cloning the Repository

```bash
# Clone with all submodules
git clone --recursive https://github.com/istio/istio.git
cd istio

# If you forgot --recursive, initialize submodules:
git submodule update --init --recursive
```

### Understanding the Build System

Istio uses a Makefile-based build system with optional Docker containerization:

- **`Makefile`**: Top-level entry point that delegates to `Makefile.core.mk`
- **`Makefile.core.mk`**: Core build rules and targets
- **`common/scripts/setup
... (truncated)
